ARIE vol.046, 1923-1924


A.--List of copper plates examined during the year 1923-24.
1
Placement
Sri. L.N.Deb, Jubraj ofTekkali.
Year
EasternGaṅga.
King
Indravarman, son of Dānār-ṇava.
Date
(Gaṅga) year154, SolarEclipse.
Language and Script
Sanskrit
Remarks
Registers the grant, by the king, of some landsin the village of Tuṅgannā in the Rūppavati-vishaya as a brahmadēya, to Skandaśarm-man of the Śāṇḍilya-gōtra and the Vājasa-nēya-śākhā, who was learned in the Vēdasand the Vēdāṅgas and who was a resident of(the village) Garakhonna, for the merit ofAchchipōḍi-Bhaṭṭārikā. The inscription wascomposed by the Sarvādhikṛita Śambapurō-pādhyāya, son of Dharmachandra, theSuperintendent of Elephants (hastyadhyak-sha) and engraved by Khaṇḍichandra, son of[Ā]ditya-Bhōgaka.
2
Placement
Sri Gopinath Deb, SecondPrince of Tekkali.
Year
Do.
King
Dēvēndravarman, son of Rājēn-dravarman.
Date
(Gaṅga) year[11]0.
Language and Script
Sanskrit
Remarks
Damaged. Registers the grant of the villagecalled Nivi[no] in the [Varāga]vartanī-vishaya, to a poet (name lost) who was theson of Mahāpratīhāra Chandavarmman, bythe king, for the merit of his parents. Theinscription was composed by Sāmanta Sarva-cha[ndra] and engraved by Sāmanta Khaṇḍi-malla.
3
Placement
The Tahsildar of Tenali
Year
EasternChāḷukya.
King
Ammarāja (I) alias Sarvalōkā-śraya Śrī Vishṇuvardhana-Mahārāja.
Date
…
Language and Script
Sanskrit
Remarks
Damaged. Gives the genealogy and the dura-tions of the reigns of the Eastern Chāḷukyakings down to the king. Registers the grantof the village Pulivaṟṟu in the Velanāṇḍu-vishaya, by the king, to Indaparāja, thegrandson of Indaparāja of the Mahāraṭṭa-vaṁśa, who was the ‘lord of the city ofMānyakhēṭa.’
4
Placement
M. R.Ry. K.Nageswara RaoPantulu Garu, Editor,Andhra Patrika, Madras.
Year
Do.
King
Sakalalōkāśraya Śrī Jayasiṁ-ghavallabha-Mahārāja.
Date
Jyēshṭha,Paurṇamāsī.Saṁkrānti.
Language and Script
Sanskrit
Remarks
Registers the grant, by the king, of the villagePeṇukapaṟu in the Karmarāshṭra to ŚrīEṟa-Drōṇaśarman, who was a resident ofVaṁgipaṟu, who was proficient in the fourVēdas and all the Śāstras, and who was theson of Dēvaśarman who had performed theSarvakratu sacrifice, and the grandson ofGuṁja-Dēvaśarman of the Kauṇḍinya-gōtra, Taittirīya-śākhā and the Āpastamba-sūtra.
5
Placement
M.R.Ry. R.VaidyanathaAyyar Avargal, B.A., DeputyCollector, Tirukkoilur, SouthArcot district.
Year
…
King
TribhuvanachakravartinKōṉēri[ṉ*]maikoṇḍāṉ.
Date
3rd year, Āṉi
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
Some plates are missing in the middle. Regis-ters the royal grant of Ulvari, remitting thetaxes on shares of land and house-sites, inratification of the kai-ōlai given to theresidents of Avanivēndarāma-chaturvēdi-maṅgalam, which was founded after theking by Aḻagāṇḍār alias Mahābali-Vāṇarā-yar, at Tirunārāyaṇapuram in VaḍagaraiRājarāja-vaḷanāḍu.
6
Placement
The Tahsildar of Shiyali,Tanjore district.
Year
…
King
…
Date
Chitrabhānu,Makara,[Ardhōdaya ?]
Language and Script
Tamil verse
Remarks
The inscription is engraved on the two sidesof a curved copper scimitar with a cup-likedepression at the head. Records the gift ofa land and a pair of golden eyes to the godŚevvēḷ-Kandaṉ (Subrahmaṇya) at Mayilāḍi,by a commander (Daḷavāy) called Raghu-nātha Śaḍakkattēvaṉ.
7
Placement
Do.
Year
MaduraNāyaka.
King
Śokkaliṅgama-Nāyaka, son ofTirumala-Nāyaka.
Date
Śaka 1595,Pramādīcha,Aṟpaśi 9, śu.Friday,daśamī.Śadaiyam,(Śatabhi-shaj).
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
Registers the agreement made, among theresidents including the pāḷaiyakārar and thenāṭṭār of the 84 villages in the two māgā-ṇams of Kūttiyapēṭṭai and Pachchaip-peru-mānallūr in Śīgāḻi-sīmai--comprising thetract between the Koḷḷiḍam (Coleroon) andthe Kāvērī in Śōḻa-maṇḍalam which is saidto have been under the authority of the king--to the effect that they would, on behalf ofthemselves and the king, collect the maga-mai tax at one nāḻi on every kalam of theproduce, for the expenses of the sacred bathand offerings of the goddess Periyanāyaki-Ammaṉ and for repairs in the temple ofTirumēṉi-Aḻagar at Vaḍamayūram aliasTirumayilāḍi.
8
Placement
The Collector of Tanjore
Year
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1615,Prajōtpatti,Tai 16,Thursday,shashṭhī,Rēvatī.
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
Registers the grant, by the residents of severalvillages, of the right of collecting themagamai tax on the merchandise passingthrough their villages, to Kumārasvāmi-Tam-birāṉ to meet the expenses of the sacred bathand offerings and repairs in the temple ofVaidyanāthasvāmi, situated in the middleof the two rivers (Ubhaya-Kāvērī, i.e., theCauvery and the Coleroon) in Rājādhirāja-vaḷanāḍu.
9
Placement
The Collector of Tanjore
Year
Pudukkoṭṭaichiefs.
King
Vijaya Raghunātha Rāya-Bādar (Rai Bahadūr ?)Toṇḍamāṉ.
Date
Śaka 1726,Kali 4905,Raktākshi,Tai 24,chaturthī,śu. Sunday,Uttiraṭṭādi,Śivanāma-yōga, Vaṇik-karaṇa.
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
Registers the gift of the village Mudalipaṭṭialias Vayittinādapuram, which was toremain under the management of Aṭchaya-liṅga-Tambirāṉ of the line of Tirujñāna-sambandha-Dēśika of the Dharmapuram-ādīnam, by the king, for certain daily andspecial services to the images of Vaidyanāthasvāmin and Taiyal Nāyaki-Ammaṉ in thetemple at Vaidīśvarankōyil. The names ofthe Vijayanagara rulers from Mallikārjuna-dēva-Mahārāya down to Śrīraṅgadēva-Mahārāya are indifferently given at thebeginning of the inscription.

224
Placement
On the south wall of the centralshrine and the west and southwalls of the maṇḍapa of theSadguṇēśvarasvāmin temple atKaruveli, Nannilam taluk,Tanjore district.
Year
Chōḷa
King
Tribhuvanachakravartin Rājādhirājadēva(II).
Date
4th year
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
Damaged. Registers the confirmation, by the Nyāyattār ofboth the Perundanam and Siṟudanam, of the grants ofland, some as Vīrabhōgam, made to the temple of Tiruk-koṭṭiṭṭai-Uḍaiyār at Karuvili alias Kulōttuṅgaśōḻanallūrin Veṇṇāḍu, a subdivision of Uyyakkoṇḍār-vaḷanāḍu, bycertain persons at different times in the reign ofKulōttuṅga-Chōḷadēva, “who abolished the tolls.” Acertain Pottappichchōḻar figures as one of the donors.Mentions the temple of Paśitāṅgīśvaram-Uḍaiyār.

Refers to the grant ofsome Vīrabhōgam (?) to the members of the Perundanamand Śiṟundanam in the 8th year of the king.

Begins with the introduction tiruman_n_ivaLara etc.Sale of a house-site to the same princess by a resident ofKalākarachchēri of the village to make up the deficit ofthe Vaidyabhōga provided (by her) for looking after thehospital called Sundaraśōḻa-Viṇṇagar Ātulaśālai atTañjāvūr.
